  <script>
        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "West Europe";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-westeurope-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script>

   <section class="section section-size7 section--gray20" id="overview" aria-label="Create innovative AI solutions" data-module="content-overview-01"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-4"> 
      <h2>Create innovative AI solutions</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-8"> 
      <p>Discover Azure AI—a portfolio of AI services designed for developers and data scientists. Take advantage of the decades of breakthrough research, responsible AI practices, and flexibility that Azure AI offers to build and deploy your own AI solutions. Access high-quality vision, speech, language, and decision-making AI models through simple API calls, and create your own machine learning models with tools like Jupyter Notebook, Visual Studio Code, and open-source frameworks like TensorFlow and PyTorch.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Dlaczego warto wybra? platform? Azure na potrzeby sztucznej inteligencji?" data-module="title-01"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-centered text-center"> 
      <h2>Dlaczego warto wybra? platform? Azure na potrzeby sztucznej inteligencji?</h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-4 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Build on your terms</h3> 
      <p>Access frameworks, tools, and capabilities for developers and data scientists of any skill level.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-4 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Deploy mission-critical AI solutions</h3> 
      <p>Use the same proven AI services that power AI capabilities in Xbox, HoloLens, and Microsoft Teams.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-4 end"> 
      <h3 class="text-heading4">Apply AI responsibly</h3> 
      <p>Get tools, services, and guidelines to help you use AI responsibly, while also preserving data privacy, transparency, and trust.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

         <div class="row column"> 
          <h3>Uczenie maszynowe</h3> 
          <p>Only Azure empowers you with the most advanced machine learning capabilities. Quickly and easily build, train, and deploy your machine learning models using <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/">Azure Machine Learning</a> and <a href="/pl-pl/services/databricks/">Azure Databricks</a>. Use the latest tools like Jupyter and Visual Studio Code, alongside frameworks like <a href="/pl-pl/develop/pytorch/">PyTorch Enterprise</a>, <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/machine-learning/how-to-train-tensorflow">TensorFlow</a>, and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/machine-learning/how-to-train-scikit-learn">Scikit-Learn</a>. Expand your data science teams and create models faster with low-code and no-code tools like <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/automatedml/">automated machine learning</a> and a <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/designer/">drag-and-drop interface</a>. Plus, easily deploy at scale with <a href="/pl-pl/services/kubernetes-service/">Azure Kubernetes Service (AKS)</a> and optimize machine learning inferencing with <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/pl-pl/azure/machine-learning/concept-onnx">ONNX Runtime</a>.</p> 
          <p><a href="/pl-pl/overview/ai-platform/data-scientist-resources/" class="arrow-link">Start building machine learning solutions today with these resources</a></p>
